***упразднить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:упразднить.html>упраздни́ть</a> (20986)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:упрашивать.html>упра́шивать</a> (12601)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упросить.html>упроси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uprosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упрашивать.html>упра́шивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uprášivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упросить.html>упроси́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to entreat, to beg, to beseech</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:упрек.html>упрек</a> (5776)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*прёк</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*prjok</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crosswise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*перёк</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*perjók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">поперёк</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poperjók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Original meaning "objection".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru">упрёк</strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uprjók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упрек.html>упрёка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упрек.html>упрёки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упрек.html>упрёков</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:упрекать.html>упрека́ть</a> (8395)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">упрёк</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uprjók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:упростить.html>упрости́ть</a> (24970)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простой.html>просто́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; less likely from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простить.html>прости́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упростить.html>упрости́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uprostítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упрощать.html>упроща́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to simplify
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упростить.html>упрости́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:задача.html>зада́чу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uprostítʹ</b> zadáču</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to simplify a problem</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упростить.html>упрости́ть</a></b> орфогра́фию</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uprostítʹ</b> orfográfiju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to simplify spelling</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to oversimplify
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упростить.html>упрости́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:смысл.html>смысл</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:событие.html>собы́тий</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uprostítʹ</b> smysl sobýtij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to oversimplify the significance of events</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упростить.html>упрости́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:идея.html>иде́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:произведение.html>произведе́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uprostítʹ</b> idéju proizvedénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to oversimplify the idea of the book</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">упроща́ться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uproščátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">упрости́ться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uprostítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">упроще́нство</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uproščénstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">упроще́нческий</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uproščénčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:упрощать.html>упроща́ть</a> (22829)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упростить.html>упрости́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uprostítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упрощать.html>упроща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uproščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упростить.html>упрости́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to simplify
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упрощать.html>упроща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:задача.html>зада́чу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uproščátʹ</b> zadáču</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to simplify a problem</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упрощать.html>упроща́ть</a></b> орфогра́фию</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uproščátʹ</b> orfográfiju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to simplify spelling</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to oversimplify
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упрощать.html>упроща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:смысл.html>смысл</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:событие.html>собы́тий</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uproščátʹ</b> smysl sobýtij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to oversimplify the significance of events</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упрощать.html>упроща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:идея.html>иде́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:произведение.html>произведе́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uproščátʹ</b> idéju proizvedénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to oversimplify the idea of the book</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***упрятать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:упрятать.html>упря́тать</a> (12658)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прятать.html>пря́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prjátatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упрятать.html>упря́тать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uprjátatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">упря́тывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hide, to take/put away</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put away, to condemn <i>(to)</i>, to confine <i>(in)</i>, to incarcerate <i>(in)</i>, to coop up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упрятать.html>упря́тать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тюрьма.html>тюрьму́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uprjátatʹ</b> v tjurʹmú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to send to prison, put away/inside</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упрятать.html>упря́тать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:психушка.html>психу́шку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uprjátatʹ</b> v psixúšku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to incarcerate [lock up; coop up] in a mental hospital</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***упускать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:упускать.html>упуска́ть</a> (10689)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пускать.html>пуска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">puskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упускать.html>упуска́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">upuskátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упустить.html>упусти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to let go, to let slip</li>
<li>to miss, to lose</li>
<li>to overlook</li></ol>

***упустить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:упустить.html>упусти́ть</a> (4059)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустить.html>пусти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pustítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упустить.html>упусти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">upustítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упускать.html>упуска́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to let go, to let slip</li>
<li>to miss, to lose</li>
<li>to overlook</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ура.html>ура́</a> (4620)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection_2">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ура.html>ура́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">urá</span>)

<ol><li>hoorah, hooray <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">elated expression of approval, especially as a battle cry</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ура.html>ура́</a></b>! <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ура.html>ура́</a></b>! <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ура.html>ура́</a></b>! донцы́ <a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сню</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:петь.html>пою́т</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Urá</b>! <b>Urá</b>! <b>Urá</b>!
